    ORDER BY [o].[Id] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_3 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_4 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a1].[Username], [a1].[Password], [o2].[Description], [o2].[Id], [a1].[Id] AS [Id0], [o2].[OrderId]

    WHERE ([o2].[Active] = 1) AND ([a1].[Active] = 1)
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[OrderId]

    FROM [OrderAccount] AS [o3]
    INNER JOIN [AccountBuy] AS [a2] ON [o3].[AccountBuyId] = [a2].[Id]
    WHERE ([o3].[Active] = 1) AND ([a2].[Active] = 1)
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[OrderId]
